Instrument Command Reference

This is the reference for all the instrument commands issued by the driver.

Instrument Commands

Instrument Command Reference
*CLS StatusClear
*ESE STATUS_STANDARD_EVENT_ENABLE_REGISTER
*ESE? STATUS_STANDARD_EVENT_ENABLE_REGISTER
*ESR? StatusStandardEventReadEventRegister
*OPC? SystemWaitForOperationComplete
*RST Disable

reset

*SRE? STATUS_SERVICE_REQUEST_ENABLE_REGISTER
*STB? StatusReadStatusByteRegister
*TST? self_test
